)@@G@@  A1,INID             . GET FIRST WORD    @E@@@@          SSL       A1,2FM
)@@G@@7               . GET FIRST CHAR    @D@@@@          TNE,U     A1,'#'    FN
)@@G@@          . POUND SIGN? @F@@@@          J         CONTROL             . FO
)@@G@@IF SO, CONTROL IMAGE    @F@@@@          AN,U      A1,060              . FP
)@@G@@IF NOT, MUST BE NUMBER  @E@@@@          TG,U      A1,1                . FQ
)@@G@@BETWEEN 1 AND 9   @ @@@@          TG,U      A1,10     @D@@@@          J FR
)@@G@@        ERRIN               . IT'S NOT    @F@@@@          TNZ       CODEFS
)@@G@@-1,A1           . IS THIS TERMINAL ACTIVE @C@@@@          J         NOTEFT
)@@G@@RM              . NO    @F@@@@          S         A1,X11              . FU
)@@G@@SAVE TERMINAL INDEX     @E@@@@          L         A1,CODE-1,A1        . FV
)@@G@@GET TERMINAL CODE @G@@@@          AN,U      A0,1                . CORRECFW
)@@G@@T FOR EXTRA WORD READ   @F@@@@          JNZ       A0,IN2              . FX
)@@G@@HANDLE IMAGE, IF ANY    @H@@@@PTBLNK    L         A0,BLANKS           . FY
)@@G@@NO, SEND A WORD OF BLANKS INSTEAD   @ @@@@          S         A0,IN     FZ
)@@G@@@D@@@@          L,U       A0,1                . ONE WORD?   @E@@@@      GA
)@@G@@    L,U       A2,IN               . SET BUFFER ADDR   @G@@@@IN2       LSGB
)@@G@@SL      A0,2                . MULT BY 4 TO GET CHAR COUNT   @F@@@@      GC
)@@G@@    S         A0,CHAR1            . STORE IN CHAR COUNT     @F@@@@      GD
)@@G@@    S         A1,TERM1            . STORE TERMINAL CODE     @E@@@@      GE
)@@G@@    S         A2,BUFF1            . STORE BUFFER ADDR @ @@@@          L,GF
)@@G@@U       A0,RSPUT$ @E@@@@          S         A0,FUNC             . SET INGG
)@@G@@PUT FUNCTION@E@@@@          L,U       A0,RSPKT            . GET RSI$ PKTGH
)@@G@@ ADDR @E@@@@          ER        RSI$                . SEND INPUT IMAGE  GI
)@@G@@@C@@@@          TP        RSPKT+2             . OK?   @F@@@@          J GJ
)@@G@@        PUTERR              . NO, HANDLE INPUT ERROR  @^@@@@          L GK
)@@G@@        A0,C@E@@@@          TEP,U     A0,020              . EXPOOL TIGHTGL
)@@G@@?     @F@@@@          J         EXPOOL              . YES, SAY SO, AND EGM
)@@G@@XIT   @F@@@@          J         0,X10               . GO BACK FOR MORE IGN
)@@G@@NPUT  @[@@@@.     @ @@@@. RSGAW$ OUTPUT ERROR ROUTINE @[@@@@.     @^@@@@GO
)@@G@@          ON        GAW @G@@@@GETERR    L,H2      A0,OUTPKT+2         . GP
)@@G@@GET TERMINAL NUMBER RETURNED  @F@@@@          TNZ       A0              GQ
)@@G@@    . ANY TERMINAL NUMBER?    @G@@@@          J         EOF             GR
)@@G@@    . NO, ALL MUST HAVE TERMINATED  @F@@@@          L,U       R1,9      GS
)@@G@@          . YES, FIND TERMINAL INDEX@ @@@@          L         X11,(1,0) GT
)@@G@@@A@@@@          SE        A0,CODE,*X11    @E@@@@          J         0,X1GU
)@@G@@0               . NO FIND, IGNORE IT@^@@@@          OFF       GAW @[@@@@GV
)@@G@@.     @G@@@@. RSPUT$ INPUT ERROR ROUTINE, AND CONTINUATION OF OUTPUT ERRGW
)@@G@@OR ROUTINE. @B@@@@. MARK INDICATED TERMINAL 'INACTIVE'.     @[@@@@.     GX
)@@G@@@F@@@@PUTERR    SZ        CODE-1,X11          . CLEAR TERMINAL CODE     GY
)@@G@@@E@@@@          SZ        A                   . CLEAR STATUS BITS @F@@@@GZ
)@@G@@          L,U       A0,' 0',X11         . FORM ASCII SITE NUMBER  @ @@@@HA
)@@G@@          S,H1      A0,STERM+1@D@@@@          L         A0,(0104,STERM) HB
)@@G@@    . GET MSG     @D@@@@          ER        APRINT$             . PRINT HC
)@@G@@IT    @F@@@@          L         A0,COUNT            . GET ACTIVE SITE COHD
)@@G@@UNT   @E@@@@          AN,U      A0,1                . DECREASE BY ONE   HE
)@@G@@@E@@@@          S         A0,COUNT            . STORE NEW COUNT   @E@@@@HF
)@@G@@          JZ        A0,EOF2             . IF NONE LEFT, EXIT@E@@@@      HG
)@@G@@    J         0,X10               . GO BACK FOR MORE  @[@@@@.     @C@@@@HH
)@@G@@. INPUT EOF, OR #E CONTROL STATEMENT ENCOUNTERED@[@@@@.     @[@@@@EOF.  HI
)@@G@@@G@@@@          TZ        TRMING              . OTHER ACT ALREADY TERMINHJ
)@@G@@G?    @D@@@@          ER        EXIT$               . YES, SO EXIT@F@@@@HK
)@@G@@          L,U       A0,1                . SET FLAG SO OTHER ACT   @E@@@@HL
)@@G@@          S         A0,TRMING           . KNOWS TO EXIT ALSO@G@@@@      HM
)@@G@@    L,U       A0,,X10             . GET INPUT/OUTPUT ACT INDICATOR@D@@@@HN
)@@G@@          TNE,U     A0,OUT1             . OUTPUT ACT? @E@@@@          J HO
)@@G@@        OEX                 . YES, SKIP TO OEX  @E@@@@          TNZ     HP
)@@G@@  COUNT               . ANY SITES LEFT?   @D@@@@          J         OEX HQ
)@@G@@                . NO, EXIT    @F@@@@          L,U       A0,RSTRA$       HR
)@@G@@    . YES, MUST TERMINATE THEM@F@@@@          S         A0,FUNC         HS
)@@G@@    . SET TERMINATE FUNCTION  @E@@@@          L,U       A0,RSPKT        HT
)@@G@@    . GET RSI$ PKT ADDR @E@@@@          ER        RSI$                . HU
)@@G@@SHUTDOWN ALL SITES@[@@@@EOF2. @ @@@@          L,U       A0,,X10   @ @@@@HV
)@@G@@          TNE,U     A0,OUT1   @^@@@@          J         OEX @A@@@@      HW
)@@G@@    L         A0,(0104,TRMERR)@C@@@@          TN        RSPKT+2         HX
)@@G@@    . OK?   @A@@@@OEX       L         A0,(0104,ATERM) @F@@@@          ERHY
)@@G@@        APRINT$             . PRINT TERMINATION STATUS@D@@@@          ERHZ
)@@G@@        EXIT$               . AND GO AWAY @[@@@@.     @F@@@@ERRIN     TZIA
)@@G@@        ASSUME              . ASSUME-INPUT FOR SITE X?@G@@@@          J IB
)@@G@@        ASMIMG              . YES, MUST BE ASSUME-IMAGE     @E@@@@      IC
)@@G@@    L         A0,(0102,('INPUTERR')) . INPUT ERROR    @ @@@@          ERID
)@@G@@        APRINT$   @E@@@@          J         INPUT               . GET MOIE
)@@G@@RE INPUT    @[@@@@.     @ @@@@. HANDLE CONTROL FUNCTIONS    @ @@@@. #L  IF
)@@G@@- LIST ACTIVE TERMINALS @ @@@@. #I  - PRINT INSTRUCTIONS    @B@@@@. #   IG
)@@G@@- INITIALIZE NEW TERMINAL (UP TO 9) @ @@@@. #1  - TERMINATE SITE #1     IH
)@@G@@@A@@@@. #9  - TERMINATE SITE #9 (ETC)     @E@@@@. #=N - ASSUME INPUT FORII
)@@G@@ SITE #N (IF 0, TURN OFF ASSUMPTION)@D@@@@. #A  - SEND THIS INPUT IMAGE IJ
)@@G@@TO ALL ACTIVE TERMINALS @ @@@@. #E  - TERMINATE PROGRAM     @[@@@@.     IK
)@@G@@@G@@@@CONTROL.                                . INITIALIZE/TERMINATE SITIL
)@@G@@ES    @G@@@@          L         A1,INID             . GET CONTROL CHARACIM
)@@G@@TERS AGAIN  @D@@@@          LSSL      A1,9                . SHIFT Q2    IN
)@@G@@@D@@@@          SSL       A1,27               . TO BOTTOM   @F@@@@      IO
)@@G@@    TNE,U     A1,'='              . ASSUME-INPUT CONTROL    @E@@@@      IP
)@@G@@    J         SETASM              . YES, HANDLE IT    @E@@@@          L,IQ
)@@G@@H2      A2,INID             . GET 2ND TWO CHARS @D@@@@          TE,U    IR
)@@G@@  A2,'  '             . BOTH BLANK  @H@@@@          J         ERRIN     IS
)@@G@@          . NO, INPUT ERROR, OR ASSUME IMAGE    @E@@@@          TNE,U   IT
)@@G@@  A1,' '              . 2ND CHAR BLANK    @E@@@@          J         NEWSIU
)@@G@@IT              . YES, INIT NEW SITE@F@@@@          TNE,U     A1,'A'    IV
)@@G@@          . INPUT TO ALL SITES?     @E@@@@          J         ALLMSG    IW
)@@G@@          . YES, HANDLE IT    @C@@@@          TNE,U     A1,'E'          IX
)@@G@@    . EXIT? @C@@@@          J         EOF                 . YES   @E@@@@IY
)@@G@@          TNE,U     A1,'L'              . LIST ACTIVE SITES @D@@@@      IZ
)@@G@@    J         LIST                . YES, DO IT  @E@@@@          TNE,U   JA
)@@G@@  A1,'S'              . SINGLE SPACE MODE?@E@@@@          J         SINGJB
)@@G@@LE              . YES, SET FLAG     @E@@@@          TNE,U     A1,'M'    JC
)@@G@@          . MULTI-SPACE MODE? @G@@@@          J         MULTI           JD
)@@G@@    . YES, CLEAR SINGLE LINE FLAG   @E@@@@          TNE,U     A1,'I'    JE
)@@G@@          . PRINT INSTRUCTIONS@C@@@@          J         PINST           JF
)@@G@@    . YES   @F@@@@          AN,U      A1,060              . NO, CHECK FOJG
)@@G@@R NUMBER    @E@@@@          TG,U      A1,1                . GREATER THANJH
)@@G@@ 0    @E@@@@          TG,U      A1,10               . AND LESS THAN 10  JI
)@@G@@@D@@@@          J         ERRIN               . NO GOOD     @E@@@@      JJ
)@@G@@    TNZ       CODE-1,A1           . TERMINAL ACTIVE   @C@@@@          J JK
)@@G@@        NOTERM              . NO    @F@@@@          L,U       A0,RSTRM$ JL
)@@G@@          . GET TERMINATE FUNCTION  @ @@@@          S         A0,FUNC   JM
)@@G@@@E@@@@          L         A0,CODE-1,A1        . GET TERMINAL CODE @E@@@@JN
)@@G@@          S         A0,TERM1            . AND STORE IN PKT  @D@@@@      JO
)@@G@@    L,U       A0,RSPKT            . GET RSI$ PKT@C@@@@          ER      JP
)@@G@@  RSI$                . DO IT @F@@@@          SZ        CODE-1,A1       JQ
)@@G@@    . CLEAR CODE FROM TABLE   @G@@@@          L         A0,COUNT        JR
)@@G@@    . GET ACTIVE TERMINAL COUNT     @D@@@@          AN,U      A0,1      JS
)@@G@@          . SUBTRACT 1  @E@@@@          S         A0,COUNT            . JT
)@@G@@STORE NEW VALUE   @E@@@@          JZ        A0,EOF              . IF NONJU
)@@G@@E LEFT, EXIT@G@@@@          L,U       A1,' 0',A1          . GET ASCII TEJV
)@@G@@RMINAL NUMBER     @ @@@@          S,H1      A1,STERM+1@A@@@@          L JW
)@@G@@        A0,(0104,STERM) @C@@@@          TP        RSPKT+2             . JX
)@@G@@OK    @B@@@@          L         A0,(0101,('ERR '))    @D@@@@          ERJY
)@@G@@        APRINT$             . PRINT MSG   @F@@@@          J         INPUJZ
)@@G@@T               . AND GO BACK FOR MORE    @]@@@@NEWSIT.     @G@@@@      KA
)@@G@@    L         A0,COUNT            . GET NUMBER OF ACTIVE TERMINALS@E@@@@KB
)@@G@@          TG,U      A0,9                . LESS THAN NINE    @G@@@@      KC
)@@G@@    J         ERRIN               . NO, CAN'T HANDLE ANY MORE     @ @@@@KD
)@@G@@          L,U       A0,RSDEM$ @F@@@@          S         A0,FUNC         KE
)@@G@@    . SET DEMAND INIT FUNCTION@F@@@@          SZ        A0              KF
)@@G@@    . SEARCH FOR OPEN SLOT    @^@@@@          L,U       R1,9@ @@@@      KG
)@@G@@    L         X11,(1,-1)@D@@@@          SE        A0,CODE+1,*X11      . KH
)@@G@@FIND ONE    @D@@@@          ER        EABT$               . IMPOSSIBLE! KI
)@@G@@@F@@@@          L         A0,SITE1            . GET ORIGINAL SITEID     KJ
)@@G@@@D@@@@          A,U       A0,,X11             . ADD INDEX   @F@@@@      KK
)@@G@@    S         A0,SITE             . STORE SITEID IN RSPKT   @ @@@@      KL
)@@G@@    L,U       A0,RSPKT  @E@@@@          ER        RSI$                . KM

)@@G@@        EABT$               . ERROR @^@@@@          L         A0,C@ @@@@KO

)@@G@@          JN        A1,ERRIN            . IF NON-NUMERIC, ERROR   @E@@@@KZ

)@@G@@    J         ERRIN     @F@@@@          JZ        A1,CLRASM           . LB

)@@G@@IS THIS SITE ACTIVE?    @C@@@@          J         NOTERM              . LD

)@@G@@. REPLACE WITH PROPER CONTROL CHAR  @D@@@@      L,Q2       A0,IN        WJ
)@@G@@  . TEST SECOND CHAR    @C@@@@      TNE,U   A0,0137    . WAS IT AND UPARWK
)@@G@@ROW   @E@@@@      S,Q2    A1,IN     . REPLACE WITH PROPER CONTROL CAHR  WL
)@@G@@@G@@@@      . THIS PORTION OF PROG WILL CHECK WETHER MORE INPUT IS NECESWM
)@@G@@SARY  @C@@@@      L       A0,COMAC  . GET CHAR COUNT AGAIN  @ @@@@      WN
)@@G@@DSL     A0,36     .     @D@@@@      DI,U    A0,4      . A0=WORD INDEX A1WO
)@@G@@=CHAR INDEX @C@@@@      EX      LOAD1,A1  . GET LAST CHAR OF INPUT@C@@@@WP
)@@G@@      TNE,U   A3,0137   . WAS IT AN UPARROW     @C@@@@      J       MOREWQ
)@@G@@      . NO THEN GET MORE INPUT@D@@@@SEND   L,U     A0,INP    . GET ADDREWR
)@@G@@SS OF RSI$ PACKET @E@@@@      ER      RSI$      . SEND IT TO EXEC FROM TWS
)@@G@@ERMINAL 1   @B@@@@      TP      INP+2     . BAD RSI$ CALL   @D@@@@      WT
)@@G@@J      TERM1               . TERM THIS SITE     @B@@@@      L       A0,IWU
)@@G@@NC    . GET STATUS BITS @B@@@@      TEP,U   A0,020    . EXPOOL TIGHT    WV
)@@G@@@B@@@@      J       EXPOOL    . SAY SO AND EXIT @F@@@@      CLEAR    IN,WW
)@@G@@20                     . CLEAR OUT INPUT BUFFER @G@@@@      CLEAR    EXTWX
)@@G@@RA,8                   . CLEAR OUT EXTRA INPUT BUFFER @B@@@@      J     WY
)@@G@@  INACT     . GO BACK FOR MORE@]@@@@      .     @]@@@@      .     @]@@@@WZ
)@@G@@      .     @G@@@@      . THIS ROUTINE WILL ISSUE ANOTHER COM$ TO GET EXXA
)@@G@@TRA IMAGES FROM   @F@@@@      . THE CONSOLE. AND PACK THE DATA INTO THE XB
)@@G@@OUTPUT BUFFER FOR @A@@@@      . RSI TO SEND TO THE EXEC     @[@@@@MORE. XC
)@@G@@@E@@@@      L       A0,COMAC  . GET OLD CHAR COUNT FROM FIRST COM$@D@@@@XD
)@@G@@      AN,U    A0,1      . SUBTRACT ONE FOR THE UPARROW@C@@@@      S     XE
)@@G@@  A0,TEMP   . SAVE FOR LATER USE    @C@@@@      L,U     A0,CONT   . GET XF
)@@G@@CONTINUE SOLICIT  @C@@@@      S       A0,COMAD  . STORE IN COM$ PACKET  XG
)@@G@@@C@@@@      L,U     A0,5      . GET OUTPUT CHAR COUNT @D@@@@      S     XH
)@@G@@  A0,COMOC  . STORE IN THE COM$ PACKET    @E@@@@      L,U     A0,EXTRA  XI
)@@G@@. GET ADRESS OF NEW INPUT BUFFER    @C@@@@      S       A0,COMID  . STORXJ
)@@G@@E INTO COM$ PACKET@B@@@@      L,U     A0,COMPK  . GET COM$ PACKET @B@@@@XK
)@@G@@      ER      COM$      . GET EXTRA INPUT @C@@@@      L       A0,COMAC  XL
)@@G@@. GET NEW CHAR COUNT    @C@@@@      JZ      A0,MORE3  . NONE THEN FORGETXM
)@@G@@ IT   @C@@@@      S       A0,R2     . STORE FOR LOOP COUNT  @C@@@@      XN
)@@G@@JGD     R1,$+1    . DECREMENT COUNT BY ONE@D@@@@      L       X9,(1,EXTRXO
)@@G@@A) . INDE FOR NEW INPUT BUFFER@D@@@@      L       A0,TEMP   . GET OLD BUXP
)@@G@@FF CHAR COUNT     @ @@@@      DSL     A0,36     .     @D@@@@      DI,U  XQ
)@@G@@  A0,4      . A0=WORD INDEX A1=CHAR INDEX @C@@@@      TNZ     A1        XR
)@@G@@. IS IT WITHIN A WORD   @E@@@@      A,U     A0,1      . SET A0 INDEX TO XS
)@@G@@THE NEXT WORD     @F@@@@      LXI,U    A0,1                      . SET IXT
)@@G@@NCREMENT ALSO     @F@@@@      LXI,U    A1,1                      . SET IXU
)@@G@@NCREMENT IN A1    @F@@@@      LXM,U     A3,0      . A3=CHAR INDEX FOR NEXV
)@@G@@W INPUT BUFFER    @G@@@@      LXI,U    A3,1                      . SET IXW
)@@G@@NCREMNT PORTION OF A3   @F@@@@MORE1 EX      LOAD,*A3  . GET CHAR FROM NEXX
)@@G@@W WORD AND PUT INTO A4  @G@@@@      EX      STORE,*A1 . STORE IN DESIGNAXY
)@@G@@TED CHAR POSITION OF OLD BUFF @C@@@@      JGD     R2,MORE1  . GET NEXT CXZ
)@@G@@HAR IN WORD @C@@@@MORE3 L       A0,COMAC  . GET NEW CHAR COUNT    @D@@@@YA
)@@G@@      AA      A0,TEMP   . ADD IT TO THE OLD CHAR COUNT@C@@@@      S     YB
)@@G@@  A0,INCH   . STORE IN RSI$ PACKET  @A@@@@      J       SEND      . SENDYC
)@@G@@ IT   @B@@@@      . ROUTINE FOR BAD IDENT RECOVERY    @]@@@@      .     YD
)@@G@@@]@@@@      .     @]@@@@      .     @]@@@@EXPOOL.     @C@@@@      L,U   YE
)@@G@@  A0,12   . EXPOOL MSG CHAR COUNT   @C@@@@      S       A0,COMOC  . STORYF
)@@G@@RE IN COM$ PACKET @D@@@@      L,U     A0,EXPMSG . GET ADDRESS OF EXPOOL YG
)@@G@@MSG   @C@@@@      S       A0,COMAD  . STORE IN COM$ PACKET  @C@@@@      YH
)@@G@@SZ      COMPK+2   . NO RESPONSE REQUIRED  @D@@@@      L,U     A0,COMPK  YI
)@@G@@. GET ADDRESS OF COM$ PACKET  @A@@@@      ER      COM$      . SEND IT   YJ
)@@G@@@]@@@@      .     @]@@@@      .     @ @@@@      .  TERMINATION FUNCTION YK
)@@G@@@[@@@@TERM1.@ @@@@      L,U     A0,1      .     @C@@@@      S       A0,TYL
)@@G@@ERMF  . SET TERM FLAG(SAFETY) @C@@@@      L,U     A0,RSTRM$ . GET TERM FYM
)@@G@@UNCTION     @C@@@@      S       A0,INFC   . STORE IN RSI$ PACKET  @C@@@@YN
)@@G@@      L,U     A0,13   . GET TERMSG CHAR COUNT   @C@@@@      S       A0,CYO
)@@G@@OMOC . STORE IN COM$ PACKET   @C@@@@      L,U     A0,TRMSG . GET ADDRESSYP
)@@G@@ OF TERM MSG@C@@@@      S       A0,COMAD  . STORE IN COM$ PACKET  @C@@@@YQ
)@@G@@      SZ      COMPK+2   . NO RESPNSE REWUIRED   @D@@@@      L,U     A0,CYR
)@@G@@OMPK  . GET ADDRESS OF COM$ PACKET  @C@@@@      ER      COM$      . TELLYS
)@@G@@ HIM HES TERMING  @B@@@@      L,U     A0,INP    . GET RSI$ PACKET @C@@@@YT
)@@G@@      ER      RSI$      . KILL THIS TERMINAL    @^@@@@      ER      EXITYU
)@@G@@$     @#@@@@      END     INIT___M$ PACKET@B@@@@      L,U     A0,COMPK  YV

)@@G@@LEMS MAY BE ENCOUNTERED IN MOVING FROM SECURE LEVEL 15 TO A @F@@@@. HIGHAP
)@@G@@ER LEVEL, IF YOU HAVE REMOVABLE DISC FILES.  ON LEVEL 15,   @E@@@@. SECUAQ
)@@G@@RE SAVED ONLY THE DIRECTORY ITEMS FOR REMOVABLE FILES.@F@@@@. THESE DIREAR
)@@G@@CTORY ITEMS WERE WRITTEN ON BACKUP TAPES ALONG WITH   @ @@@@. THE BACKUPAS
)@@G@@S OF FIXED FILES. @[@@@@.     @G@@@@. AS OF LEVEL 16, SECURE IS CAPABLE AT
)@@G@@OF SAVING THE TEXT OF REMOVABLE     @F@@@@. FILES, AND NO LONGER DOES THAU
)@@G@@IS DIRECTORY-ONLY STUFF FOR THEM.   @G@@@@. ALSO, IT WILL NOT TOUCH A REAV
)@@G@@MOVABLE FILE AT ALL UNLESS SPECIFICALLY   @F@@@@. INSTRUCTED TO DO SO VIAW
)@@G@@A A 'SAVE PACK XXX' OR 'SAVE FILE XXX'    @]@@@@. COMMAND.  @[@@@@.     AX
)@@G@@@F@@@@. THEREFORE, ALL THOSE DIRECTORY ITEMS THAT SECURE 15 LEFT LYING  AY
)@@G@@@F@@@@. AROUND ALL OVER YOUR BACKUP TAPES WILL STAY THERE FOREVER (AND  AZ
)@@G@@@E@@@@. THE REELS WILL BE LISTED AS ACTIVE TAPES), UNLESS YOU DO A@F@@@@BA
)@@G@@. 'SAVE ALL PACKS' OR THE EQUIVALENT.  ('SAVE ALL' WON'T TOUCH    @E@@@@BB
)@@G@@. REMOVABLE DISC FILES).  ALSO, IF YOU USE A 'MERGE' PROGRAM@G@@@@. SUCHBC
)@@G@@ AS THE ONE IN THIS FILE, WHICH GENERATES 'SAVE ALL FILE XXX'     @F@@@@BD
)@@G@@. COMMANDS FOR EACH FILE FOUND TO BE BACKED UP ON A GIVEN TAPE,   @F@@@@BE
)@@G@@. YOU MAY WIND UP SAVING THE TEXT OF REMOVABLE FILES WHEN YOU     @^@@@@BF
)@@G@@. DIDN'T WANT TO DO SO. @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. THE BEST THING TO DO WHEN MOBG
)@@G@@VING FROM SECURE 15 TO A HIGHER     @F@@@@. LEVEL WOULD BE TO MARK ALL TBH
)@@G@@HE REMOVABLE FILES AS 'NOT BACKED   @E@@@@. UP', BUT, ALAS AND ALACK, THBI
)@@G@@ERE IS CURRENTLY NO METHOD FOR@D@@@@. CLEARING THE 'BACKED UP' BIT IN A BJ
)@@G@@FILE'S MAIN ITEM. @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. THE ONLY WORKABLE METHOD WE HAVE FBK
)@@G@@OUND TO CLEAR UP THIS MESS IS @ @@@@. THE PROGRAM BELOW, WHICH:   @[@@@@BL
)@@G@@.     @F@@@@.         1. SCANS THE DIRECTORY (USING DIREC$), TO FIND EVEBM
)@@G@@RY    @^@@@@.            FILE WHICH @C@@@@.            A. IS A REMOVABLEBN
)@@G@@ DISC FILE, AND   @A@@@@.            B. HAS A BACKUP, AND   @G@@@@.     BO
)@@G@@       C. THE BACKUP IS ZERO TRACKS IN LENGTH (HOPEFULLY MEANING  @B@@@@BP
)@@G@@.               LAST SAVED BY SECURE 15). @G@@@@.         2. THE PROGRAMBQ
)@@G@@ THEN MARKS EACH SUCH FILE AS BEING BACKED UP   @G@@@@.            ON SUBR
)@@G@@CCESIVE POSITIONS OF AN IMAGINARY TAPE CALLED 'RDISC'.@[@@@@.     @F@@@@BS
)@@G@@.      (SINCE THIS PROGRAM DOES DBACK$'S OF FILES, IT MUST BE RUN @ @@@@BT
)@@G@@.      IN A PRIVILEGED RUN.)  @[@@@@.     @#@@@@          AXR$    @F@@@@BU
)@@G@@FIRST     EQU       0                   . STARTING FILE POSITION  @G@@@@BV
)@@G@@PKT       + 031                         . MSCON$ DBACK$ PACKET          BW

)@@G@@  1                   . ERROR CODE STORAGE@^@@@@ECODE     RES       2   HW

)@@G@@$(1)  @E@@@@ST        LMJ       X11,DIRINT          . INITIALIZE DIREC$ ID

)@@G@@        0   @F@@@@          TN        MAIN+11             . DISABLED IN IJ

)@@G@@@F@@@@          AND,U     A4,034              . AND OUT BITS 34 AND 32  IM
)@@G@@@D@@@@          TE,U      A5,010              . JUST BIT 33?@E@@@@      IN
)@@G@@    J         SEC                 . NO, GO GET NEXT   @F@@@@          E$IO
)@@G@@DIT     EPK                 . YES, GO GET FILE NAME   @E@@@@          E$IP
)@@G@@MSG     USE                 . FORM  USE IMAGE   @ @@@@          E$FD2   IQ
)@@G@@  MAIN+1    @^@@@@          E$CHAR    '*' @ @@@@          E$FD2     MAINIR
)@@G@@+3    @^@@@@          E$CHAR    '(' @A@@@@          E$DECV    MAIN+17,,TIS

)@@G@@          ER        CSF$                . SUBMIT  USE IMAGE @ @@@@      IW
)@@G@@    L,U       A0,ASG    @E@@@@          ER        CSF$                . IX

)@@G@@STATUS@D@@@@          TP        A0                  . STATUS OK?  @D@@@@IZ
)@@G@@          J         EXPLN               . NO, EXPLAIN @ @@@@          L,JA
)@@G@@U       A0,PKT    @#@@@@  ON  DEBUG=0     @D@@@@          ER        MSCOJB
)@@G@@N$              . DO DBITS$   @C@@@@          JN        A0,MSCNER       JC

)@@G@@NPKT+2@ @@@@          L,U       A0,SNPKT  @ @@@@          ER        SNAPJE

)@@G@@USES DIREC$ TO SEARCH THE MASTER FILE DIRECTORY, THEN PRODUCES    @F@@@@KA
)@@G@@. A LIST OF ALL @SECURE BACKUP TAPES CURRENTLY IN USE, AND AN     @D@@@@KB
)@@G@@. ALPHABETICALLY SORTED LIST OF ALL CATALOGUED FILES. @[@@@@.     @C@@@@KC
)@@G@@. THE BUFFER THAT GETS SORTED LOOKS LIKE THIS:  @[@@@@.     @G@@@@.     KD
)@@G@@     .............................................................@G@@@@KE
)@@G@@.     0    :                         QUALIFIER                         :KF
)@@G@@@G@@@@.     1    :                                                      KG
)@@G@@     :@G@@@@.          .................................................KH
)@@G@@............@G@@@@.     2    :                         FILENAME         KI
)@@G@@                 :@G@@@@.     3    :                                    KJ
)@@G@@                       :@G@@@@.          ...............................KK
)@@G@@..............................@G@@@@.     4    :  MEDIA  : INHIBIT :  LEKL
)@@G@@AD   :  PCHAR  :      F-CYCLE      :@G@@@@.          :         :  FLAGS KM
)@@G@@ :  CHAR   :         :                   :@G@@@@.          .............KN
)@@G@@................................................@G@@@@.     5    :      KO
)@@G@@   GRAN COUNT (FOR TAPE FILES, NO. OF REELS)         :@G@@@@.          .KP
)@@G@@............................................................@G@@@@.     KQ
)@@G@@6    :                        BACKUP TAPE                        :@G@@@@KR
)@@G@@.          .............................................................KS
)@@G@@@G@@@@.     7    :       BACKUP POSITION       :     BACKUP TAPE BLOCKS KT
)@@G@@     :@G@@@@.          .................................................KU
)@@G@@............@G@@@@.     8    :          BACKUP CREATION TIME, IN TDATE$ KV
)@@G@@FORMAT           :@G@@@@.          .....................................KW
)@@G@@........................@G@@@@.     9    :                          PACKKX
)@@G@@-ID                          :@G@@@@.          .........................KY
)@@G@@....................................@[@@@@.     @[@@@@.     @^@@@@AO    KZ
)@@G@@    EQU       014 @^@@@@DEBUG     EQU       0   $ @@@@-2                LA
)@@G@@      @@@@@@@H@@@@NBAKS     EQU       150                 . MAX NUMBER OLB
)@@G@@F SECURE BACKUP REELS   @G@@@@NREC      EQU       3000                . LC

)@@G@@1L    @G@@@@          S         A1,*CALLSORTF+1     . TELL SORTF HOW MANMB

)@@G@@@ @@@@          PRINT     'R$OPN '  @G@@@@          J         ROPN$     ML
)@@G@@          . OPEN SORT, RETURN TO FPOC     @[@@@@FPOC .@^@@@]          PRMM

)@@G@@6 = 0 @^@@@]. . SORT: PASS TO RREL$ @B@@@]. . NXSEC: ANY MORE SECTORS THMP

)@@G@@T TAPE(ASSUMES THAT THE TAPE  @G@@@@ .            IS NOT OVERWRITTEN).  WE
)@@G@@IN THIS CASE THE 3-LINE MESSAGE     @F@@@@ .            FOR EACH FILE ISWF
)@@G@@ DIRECTED TO THE PRINTER RATHER     @A@@@@ .            THAN THE CONSOLEWG
)@@G@@.     @[@@@@ .    @[@@@@ .    @B@@@@ .                        O P T I O WH
)@@G@@N S   @[@@@@ .    @A@@@@ .       'O' - TAPE IS OVERWRITTEN  @A@@@@ .    WI
)@@G@@   'B' - TAPE HAS A BADLABEL  @B@@@@ .       'J' - LIST ALL FILES ON TAPWJ
)@@G@@E     @[@@@@ .    @[@@@@ .    @G@@@@ . UPON STARTING THE RUN YOU WILL BEWK
)@@G@@ ASKED THE FOLLOWING QUESTIONS:     @[@@@@ .    @[@@@@ .    @B@@@@ .    WL
)@@G@@  1) KEY IN REEL NUMBER TO BE READ  @F@@@@ .           GIVE IT THE NUMBEWM
)@@G@@R OF THE OVERWRITTEN TAPE, ONLY ONE @G@@@@ .           TAPE NUMBER WILL WN

)@@G@@ BEING USED MESSAGE 1 WILL BE DISPLAYED AGAIN.  @E@@@@ .           IF THWP
)@@G@@ERE ARE NOMORE TAPES ANSWER 'NOMORE'.     @[@@@@ .    @[@@@@ .    @C@@@@WQ
)@@G@@ .      2)LOAD XXXXXX ON SS/UU   -A- OR -N-     @G@@@@ .           THIS WR
)@@G@@MESSAGE IS DISPLAYED AFTER A RESPONSE TO MESSAGE 1    @H@@@@ .          WS
)@@G@@ HAS BEEN RECEIVED. 'A' CAUSES THE INPUT TAPE TO BE SEARCHED.     @H@@@@WT
)@@G@@ .           IF THE WRONG TAPE IS MOUNTED A MESSAGE SAYING 'YOU ASKED FOWU
)@@G@@R     @G@@@@ .           XXXX AND MOUNTED YYYY' WILL BE DISPLAYED, THE IWV
)@@G@@NPUT TAPE   @D@@@@ .           WILL BE FREE'D AND MESSAGE 1 WILL APPEAR.WW
)@@G@@@H@@@@ .           'N' CAUSES THE TAPE TO BE FREE'D AND MESSAGE 1 TO BE WX
)@@G@@DISPLAYED.  @[@@@@ .    @[@@@@ .    @H@@@@ . THE INPUT TAPE IS THEN SEARWY
)@@G@@CHED UNTIL A GOOD FILE IS FOUND AFTER THE END   @H@@@@ . OF THE OVERWRITWZ
)@@G@@TEN PART OF THE TAPE. A 3 LINE MESSAGE IS THEN DISPLAYED    @A@@@@ . WITXA
)@@G@@H THE FOLLOWING INFORMATION.  @[@@@@ .    @[@@@@ .    @F@@@@ .      3) FXB
)@@G@@ILE  QUAL*FILE(CYCLE)   BACKUP NO.    POSITION: NN    @E@@@@ .         CXC
)@@G@@REATED ON MM/DD/YY AT HH:MM:SS IS A GOOD FILE   @D@@@@ .        0-IS FILXD
)@@G@@E TO BE SAVED OR SKIPPED     YNSR?  @[@@@@ .    @[@@@@ .    @F@@@@ .    XE
)@@G@@       A 'Y' RESPONSE COPIES THE FILE TO THE OUTPUT TAPE.   @G@@@@ .    XF

)@@G@@ REISSUED.  IF THE TAPE IS THE PROPER TAPE,     @D@@@@ IT IS REWOUND TO DL
)@@G@@LOAD POINT AND WRITTEN ON AS NORMAL.@#@@@@4UTILITY PROGRAMS @F@@@@      DM
)@@G@@AT UHMC, THE OPERATORS ARE RESPONSIBLE FOR THE DAY TO DAY   @G@@@@ RUNNIDN
)@@G@@NG OF @SECURE SAVES AND GENERAL UPKEEP OF THE FILES.  WE HAVE     @F@@@@DO

)@@G@@ MANY OF THESE ARE SIMPLE @SECURE RUNSTREAMS, OTHERS CREATE SECURE@E@@@@DQ

)@@G@@@G@@@@      THE SYMBOLICS OF MANY OF THE PROGRAMS ARE IN THIS FILE, WHILDS
)@@G@@E     @G@@@@ THE RUNSTREAMS AND ABSOLUTES CAN BE FOUND IN THE SYS$*RUN$ DT
)@@G@@FILE ON     @F@@@@ THIS TAPE.  MORE COMPLETE DOCUMENTATION CAN BE OBTAINDU
)@@G@@ED BY CREA- @F@@@@ TING A FILE OPERATIONS*DOC/TOR/NO FROM THE PROPER FILDV
)@@G@@E ON THIS   @F@@@@ TAPE, AND USING THE 'OPDOC' RUNSTREAM IN THE SYS$*RUNDW
)@@G@@$ FILE OF   @]@@@@ THIS TAPE. @[@@@@3ZZZAP@G@@@@      CREATES SECURE SOUDX
)@@G@@RCE STATEMENTS FOR OUTPUT OPERATIONS (SAVE,     @F@@@@ UNLOAD, REMOVE). DY
)@@G@@ LEADS THE OPERATOR THORUGH, ASKING QUESTIONS   @ @@@@ ABOUT WHAT HE WANDZ
)@@G@@TS TO DO.   @[@@@@3PAZZZ@G@@@@      AS ITS NAME IMPLIES, PAZZZ IS THE OPEA

)@@G@@ADING OR REGISTERING FILES THAT     @C@@@@ ARE NOT CATALOGUED (USES LOADEC
)@@G@@ FROM IBACKUP).   @]@@@@3ROLBAK     @D@@@@      USED TO LOAD UNLOADED (BED
)@@G@@UT CATALOGUED) FILES.   @[@@@@3LOAD @G@@@@      USED TO LOAD AN ENTIRE TEE
)@@G@@APE OR TAPES.  ASKS THE OPERATOR WHAT     @F@@@@ TAPES HE WANTS TO USE, EF
)@@G@@THEN USES DIREC$ TO SEARCH THE DIRECTORY  @F@@@@ AND CREATE 'LOAD FILE XEG
)@@G@@XX' CARDS FOR EACH FILE ON THAT TAPE SET. @F@@@@ NOTE THAT THIS IS FOR FEH

)@@G@@REGISTER (SEE 3TAPES).  @[@@@@3MERGE@G@@@@      A SECURE TAPE MERGER.  AEJ
)@@G@@SKS THE OPERATOR WHAT TAPES TO MERGE,     @F@@@@ THEN USES DIREC$ TO FINEK
)@@G@@D EACH FILE BACKED UP ON THOSE TAPES.  IT @F@@@@ THEN CREATES A 'SAVE ALEL
)@@G@@L FILE XXX' CARD FOR EACH OF THESE FILES. @]@@@@33TAPES     @F@@@@      EM
)@@G@@A MULTI-ACTIVITY SECURE EXECUTION.  ASSIGNS THREE IBACKUP   @G@@@@ TAPESEN
)@@G@@, AND DOES A 'LOAD UNTIL UEF = 45' - VERY USEFUL AFTER A FULL     @D@@@@EO
)@@G@@ BOOT, AND AFTER THE DIRECTORY TAPE IS REGISTERED.    @]@@@@3PAKREG     EP

)@@G@@@F@@@@ LONG AND STARTS WITH 'PK'.  WITH A CONDITION WORD OF 1, IT WILL  ES

)@@G@@ABLED FILE RECOVERER.  USES DIREC$ TO SEARCH THE@G@@@@ DIRECTORY FOR HAREU

)@@G@@R     @F@@@@      REGISTERS A DIRECTORY TAPE OR EVERYTHING ON A BACKUP TEZ
)@@G@@APE.  @B@@@@ ASKS THE OPERATOR WHICH HE WANTS TO DO.  @]@@@@3ROLOUT     FA

)@@G@@ WANT @]@@@@ TO UNLOAD. @[@@@@3PRT  @F@@@@      SORT OF A 'LIST REELS' CFE

)@@G@@OPMFD - CONSOLE @MFD UTILITY PROGRAM@[@@_@C     @D@@_@C     ASKS OPERATOHX
)@@G@@R WHAT HE WANTS AN @MFD LISTING OF  @F@@_@C     (PROJ, ACCT, QUAL, PACK,HY
)@@G@@ OR ALL) AND GENERATES THE PROPER   @E@@_@C     @MFD CALL.  IF RESPONSE HZ
)@@G@@IS 'ALL', SYS$*RUN$.MFDADD IS @#@@_@C     @ADD'ED.    @[@@_@C     @ @@@@IA
)@@G@@      IMPLICIT INTEGER (A-Z)  @F@@@@      DIMENSION MSG1(6), CHOICE(5), IB
)@@G@@L(4), ANS(2), MFD(4), MSG2(2),@A@@_@     *     LINE(4), FOUR(2), ASG4(2)IC
)@@G@@@G@@@@      DATA MSG1/'PROJ, ACCT, QUAL, PACK, OR ALL?'/, FOUR/'@ADD 4. ID
)@@G@@.'/,  @G@@@@     *     CHOICE/'PROJ  ACCT  QUAL  PACK  ALL   '/,L/'P','AIE
)@@G@@','Q','K'/, @F@@@@     *     MFD/'@ADD SYS$*RUN$.MFDADD '/, MSG2/'WHAT@ IF
)@@G@@XXXX?'/,    @F@@_@     *     LINE/'@MFD, P                 '/,ASG4/'@ASGIG
)@@G@@,T 4. .'/   @[@@_@C     @[@@_@C     @H@@_@1     CALL COM(31,MSG1,4,ANS,IIH
)@@G@@N)             @ ASK OPERATOR WHAT HE WANTS     @H@@_@      DO 2  I = 1,II
)@@G@@4                          @ CHECK FOR PROJ/ACCT/QUAL/PACK  @F@@_@2     IJ
)@@G@@IF (ANS(1) .EQ. CHOICE(I)) GO TO 5     @ IF SO, GO TO 5     @G@@_@      IK
)@@G@@IF (ANS(1) .NE. CHOICE(5)) GO TO 1     @ IF NOT 'ALL', TRY AGAIN  @G@@_@IL
)@@G@@      CALL CSF(MFD)                          @ @ADD SYS$*RUN$.MFDADD    IM
)@@G@@@]@@@@      STOP  @[@@_@C     @C@@_@C     RESPONSE WAS PROJ, ACCT, QUAL,IN
)@@G@@ OR PACK    @[@@_@C     @G@@_@5     CALL CSF(ASG4)                      IO
)@@G@@   @ @ASG OUTPUT FILE '4'     @H@@_@      LINE(2) = L(I)                IP
)@@G@@         @ SET CORRECT OPTION IN @MFD CALL@G@@_@      FLD(0,24,MSG2(2)) IQ
)@@G@@= FLD(0,24,ANS(1))   @ SET UP 'WHAT XXX?' MSG   @I@@_@6     IF (I .EQ. 4IR
)@@G@@) GO TO 7                  @ IF PACK, ANSWER SHOULD BE 6 CHARS    @G@@_@IS
)@@G@@      CALL COM(11,MSG2,12,ANS,IN)            @ ASK OP FOR PROJ/ACCT/QUALIT
)@@G@@@#@@@@      GO TO 8     @F@@_@7     CALL COM(11,MSG2,6,ANS,IN)          IU
)@@G@@   @ ASK OP FOR PACK    @G@@_@8     IF (IN.LT. 1) GO TO 6               IV
)@@G@@   @ IF NO REPLY, ASK AGAIN   @H@@_@      LINE(3) = ANS(1)              IW
)@@G@@         @ STORE RSPONSE IN @MFD CALL     @G@@_@      IF (IN.GT. 6) LINEIX
)@@G@@(4) = ANS(2)         @ GET 2ND WORD, IF ANY     @H@@_@      WRITE (4,9) IY
)@@G@@LINE                       @ PUT @MFD CALL IN OUTPUT FILE   @#@@@@9     IZ
)@@G@@FORMAT (4A6)@F@@_@      ENDFILE 4                              @ CLOSE OJA
)@@G@@UTPUT FILE  @F@@_@      CALL CSF(FOUR)                         @ @ADD OUJB
)@@G@@TPUT FILE   @]@@@@      STOP  @]@@@@      END   ___ @3 C)B*)CDIES*AC(^@)JC
